        jQuery.ajax({
            url: '/api/google_tokensignin.php',

function touchSlider(){
	var width = window.innerWidth;
	if(767 >= width && 567 < width){
		var swiper = new Swiper('.swiper-container', {
			loop:true,
			slidesPerView: 4,
			limitRotation: false,
			grabCursor: true
		});
	}
	if(566 >= width){
		var swiper = new Swiper('.swiper-container', {
			loop:true,
			slidesPerView: 3,
			limitRotation: false,
			grabCursor: true
		});
	}
}

touchSlider();
$(window).resize(touchSlider);
